These snatch straps can save your bacon.\\u003c/p\\u003e","short_title":"The Best Recovery Straps for Off-Roading Mishaps","index_title":"Keep the Rubber-Side Down With These Recovery Straps","introductory_text":"\\u003cp\\u003eRecovery straps\xe2\x80\x94sometimes referred to as snatch straps\xe2\x80\x94are one of many interfaces used to yank \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/cars/g38272152/best-traction-boards/\\"\\u003eyour vehicle out of a sticky situation\\u003c/a\\u003e. Many recovery straps look identical to tow straps. However, there\xe2\x80\x99s an important distinction: Recovery straps are elastic and stretch before becoming taught, whereas tow straps will simply load up until they snap. The former helps you easily get back on solid ground with minimal other equipment.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eOften compared with kinetic recovery ropes, recovery straps have their inherent advantages and disadvantages. Compared to ropes, they fold down much smaller but are often more difficult to shop for, not to mention quite a bit weaker if used improperly.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp class=\\"body-tip\\"\\u003ePrepared to Go Anywhere: \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/cars/trucks/a37806167/overland-expo-west-2021-accessories-apparel/\\"\\u003eThe Best Accessories at Overland Expo 2021\\u003c/a\\u003e \xe2\x80\xa2 \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/cars/g30460044/car-emergency-kit/\\"\\u003eWhat to Have in You Car\xe2\x80\x99s Emergency Kit\\u003c/a\\u003e \xe2\x80\xa2 \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/cars/g37023639/best-portable-tire-inflators/\\"\\u003e10 Portable Tire Inflators\\u003c/a\\u003e \xe2\x80\xa2 \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/cars/g38293716/best-portable-jump-starters/\\"\\u003eKeep It Juiced With These Portable Jump Starters\\u003c/a\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch3 class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003eWhat to Consider\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003ch4 class=\\"body-h4\\"\\u003eElasticity \\u003c/h4\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eWhen talking about a lot of recovery gear, enthusiasts will often throw around the terms kinetic and non-kinetic. Although off-road jargon can become overwhelming in a hurry, don\xe2\x80\x99t panic. There\xe2\x80\x99s one hard and fast rule you should follow when using elastic recovery straps, which are able to stretch and store kinetic energy: Never use them in a winch job, where they are under load for extended periods of time. Because kinetic straps behave like rubber bands, they can do a lot of damage if they snap. Despite this danger, the inherent stretch of a recovery strap allows the material to load up until its limit of elasticity before returning to the original compressed state. This allows for much simpler vehicle-to-vehicle recovery operations that don\xe2\x80\x99t require the complex equipment needed for a proper winching operation.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch4 class=\\"body-h4\\"\\u003eYou Get What You Pay For\\u003c/h4\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eJust like many things in life, spending more money on recovery straps leads to a better end product. When it comes to heavily strung components like these that can cause horrendous injury in the event of a failure, it\xe2\x80\x99s a good idea to stray away from cheaper straps made by brands you\xe2\x80\x99ve never heard of. You\xe2\x80\x99ll see below that even for the budget pick, we didn\xe2\x80\x99t stray below $40.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch4 class=\\"body-h4\\"\\u003eLoad Ratings\\u003c/h4\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eThe failure point for a lot of \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/cars/trucks/how-to/g1467/0-gear-essentials-for-going-off-road/\\"\\u003eoff-road equipment\\u003c/a\\u003e is generally listed as the minimum breaking strength (MBS). Although you\xe2\x80\x99d expect to hear the word maximum instead of minimum, MBS is essentially a measure to find the weakest section of any given strap\xe2\x80\x94the weakest link, if you will. Either way, a good rule of thumb is to look for an MBS that\xe2\x80\x99s roughly three times greater than the weight of your vehicle. \\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch3 class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003eHow We Selected\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eAs \\u003cem\\u003ePop Mech\\u003c/em\\u003e\xe2\x80\x99s autos editor, I\xe2\x80\x99ve taken my fair share of vehicles off-road and am rapidly working my way through the all-terrain learning curve. Tool belt suspenders prevent this from happening, and transfer much of the weight of your tools to your shoulders instead of your waist and lower back. They\xe2\x80\x99re also designed with maximum comfort in mind, and are easy to adjust to your specific height and body type.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch3 class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003eWhat to Consider\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eIt might sound obvious, but when choosing a pair of tool belt suspenders, think about what you\xe2\x80\x99d like them to do. Apart from holding up your tool belt, some options provide additional storage for items you\'d like to keep easily accessible, incorporating cell phone pockets or pencil sleeves into their design. Others utilize high-visibility colors and reflectors, making them valuable for those who work in low-light conditions. \\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eYou should also think about how much support you\xe2\x80\x99ll need. While most use a standard four-point support system\xe2\x80\x94with two clips in the front and two in the back\xe2\x80\x94others offer five points for extra support. Or, if you\xe2\x80\x99ll be carrying a relatively light load, three-point suspenders may be ideal, and can cut down on unnecessary bulk. \\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eThe material the suspenders are made from is another important factor to consider. While leather options are typically less bulky and more durable over time, they do tend to be more expensive than other types, so keep that in mind. for Outdoor Fun This Winter","index_title":"10 Best Sleds for Winter Fun","introductory_text":"\\u003cp\\u003eAfter a big snowstorm, there\xe2\x80\x99s nothing like making fresh tracks sledding down the steepest hill in your neighborhood. It\xe2\x80\x99s a relatively inexpensive winter activity, but choosing among the plastic toboggans and snow tubes and old-school \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/home/how-to-plans/how-to/g2321/how-to-build-a-steerable-sled/\\" target=\\"_blank\\"\\u003ewooden sleds\\u003c/a\\u003e on the market can be a tougher decision than you might expect. We\xe2\x80\x99ve rounded up the best sleds out there, so read on for our top recommendations, plus safety tips and things to consider before you shop. (Also, we encourage you to check out our fun read on the \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/adventure/sports/g1377/a-brief-history-of-the-sled/\\"\\u003e\\u003cu\\u003ebrief history of sledding\\u003c/u\\u003e\\u003c/a\\u003e.)\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch3 class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003eWhat to Consider\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003e\\u003c/strong\\u003eThere\xe2\x80\x99s no \xe2\x80\x9cbest\xe2\x80\x9d sled style, but rather a long list of options to consider based on personal preference, kids\' ages, whether the sled is for one or a group, and budget. The most popular types are wooden sleds (think: the classic Flexible Flyer) and disks or flying saucers, along with toboggans and snow tubes, which typically have a tow rope. There are also specialty sleds, like ski sleds\xe2\x80\x94a seat with a steering wheel set on a pair of metal runners\xe2\x80\x94and stand-up scooter sleds, which are essentially snowboards with handlebars. \\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eGenerally speaking, sleds are made from either a combination of wood and steel, plastic, or vinyl and rubber for snow tubes. Wooden sleds are treated to be water-resistant and some of the heavier plastic models are made of high-density polyethylene, often coated to prevent cracks and to ensure a smooth glide through the snow. You should also factor in a sled\xe2\x80\x99s weight, as you\xe2\x80\x99ll have to haul it back uphill.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch4 class=\\"body-h4\\"\\u003eSafety\\u003c/h4\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eIt\xe2\x80\x99s crucial to follow guidelines for \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.nsc.org/community-safety/safety-topics/seasonal-safety/winter-safety/sledding\\"\\u003e\\u003cu\\u003esledding safety\\u003c/u\\u003e\\u003c/a\\u003e\xe2\x80\x94adults included. Kids should always wear a helmet while sledding; a ski helmet is ideal, but a \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/adventure/outdoors/g3045/best-bike-helmets/\\" target=\\"_blank\\"\\u003ebike helmet\\u003c/a\\u003e is sufficient. presence of speakers by \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/technology/audio/g38150148/best-ceiling-speaker/\\"\\u003einstalling a set in walls or ceilings\\u003c/a\\u003e, says Micah specializing in audio and other consumer tech. Although built-in speakers can be outstanding, the detail and realism of good tower speakers is almost always preferable for music enthusiasts, not to mention free-standing speakers are easier to add to your living space.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch3 class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003eHow to Choose the Right Tower Speakers\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eTwo- vs. Three-Way Speakers: \\u003c/strong\\u003eYou\xe2\x80\x99ll need to decide between a two-way or three-way speaker. \xe2\x80\x9cA two-way speaker sends the high tones to a tweeter and the low and mid tones to a woofer,\xe2\x80\x9d explains Carl Prouty, a technologist at \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.abt.com/\\" target=\\"_blank\\" rel=\\"nofollow\\"\\u003eAbt Electronics\\u003c/a\\u003e in Illinois. \xe2\x80\x9cThree-way speakers incorporate mid-sized drivers to handle the mid tones and send the low tones to a subwoofer.\xe2\x80\x9d The mid-sized driver and subwoofer make for a richer audio experience.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eTwo-way speakers tend to be more affordable, and Prouty recommends them if you already have, or you intend to purchase, a separate subwoofer. \xe2\x80\x9cBut if you\xe2\x80\x99re using these speakers more for music, a three-way is a great choice as they already have a subwoofer built in,\xe2\x80\x9d he says.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eAnd in case you\xe2\x80\x99re thinking of purchasing a single speaker, that\xe2\x80\x99s generally a bad idea. \xe2\x80\x9cUsing a single speaker will only provide half the audio, which is a very bad experience and definitely not recommended,\xe2\x80\x9d Prouty says. You can purchase powered floor-standing speakers that don\xe2\x80\x99t need an amp, but in most cases, he says they won\xe2\x80\x99t provide the quality of sound you\xe2\x80\x99d get from using a separate amplifier.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eAudio Quality: \\u003c/strong\\u003eSpeaker sensitivity (or sound pressure level), as measured in decibels, is another factor to consider. But keep in mind that a higher sensitivity rating doesn\xe2\x80\x99t guarantee the best sound. The combination of many features is what determines sound quality, including the size and shape of tweeters (like cones or domes), materials (such as silk or aluminum), woofer size, frequency response, and even the cabinet quality.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eSheveloff recommends manufacturers, such as Klisch, Polk Audio, and others, that have been making excellent speakers for decades. \xe2\x80\x9cThese brands are renowned for applying innovative solutions that improve the experience for the listener,\xe2\x80\x9d he says. \xe2\x80\x9cDriver materials, cabinet construction, port designs\xe2\x80\x94these are all factors that engineers toil over to ensure best possible resolution.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eAnd when in doubt, try it out. \xe2\x80\x9cBecause each human ear is different and each listening room presents its own challenges, finding a way to audition tower speakers is the best way to make an informed buying decision,\xe2\x80\x9d Sheveloff says. \xe2\x80\x9cSome online retailers offer flexible in-home audition policies that enable consumers to comfortably make an informed choice.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u003cbr\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch3 class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eHow We Selected\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eI\xe2\x80\x99ve tested and written about tech and home products for a variety of digital publications, including \\u003cem\\u003eArchitectural Digest\\u003c/em\\u003e, \\u003cem\\u003eCNN Underscored,\\u003c/em\\u003e \\u003cem\\u003eTom\xe2\x80\x99s Guide\\u003c/em\\u003e,\\u003cem\\u003e Bob Vila\\u003c/em\\u003e, \\u003cem\\u003ePopular Science\\u003c/em\\u003e, \\u003cem\\u003eThe Spruce\\u003c/em\\u003e, \\u003cem\\u003eRealtor.com\\u003c/em\\u003e, \\u003cem\\u003eApartment Therapy\\u003c/em\\u003e, and\\u003cem\\u003e The Daily Beast\\u003c/em\\u003e. This list includes floor-standing speakers that I\xe2\x80\x99ve tested, as well as brand and individual speakers recommended by our experts, Carl Prouty and Micah Sheveloff, combined with extensive research on each of these products. often known as free weights, are the unsung heroes of the strength-training world. What they lack in heavyweight, gym-bro flash, as compared to barbells or weight plates, they more than make up for in versatility, portability, ability to do targeted strength work, and more.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eWith dumbbells, you can not only isolate specific muscle groups through basic moves like bicep curls or shoulder presses, but you can also do full-body HIIT workouts and add more resistance to functional workouts like jumping jacks and walking lunges.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eBut the best thing about dumbbells is simply their compact size\xe2\x80\x94which makes it easy to create a variety of movement patterns, like pushing, pulling, and swinging, says Katie Hake, a trainer and registered dietician in Indianapolis. \xe2\x80\x9cDumbbells allow for greater range of motion while improving coordination and muscular imbalances,\xe2\x80\x9d Hake says. \xe2\x80\x9cThey are also easy to store, which makes them a great class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eWhat to Consider When Shopping for Dumbbells\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eFirst, a little history: Dumbbells were among the first dedicated fitness tools, dating all the way back to ancient Greece. They took their current name from more recent usage in the 1700s, when church bells were used as strength-training weights once the clappers, or ringing parts inside the bell, had been removed. Today\xe2\x80\x99s dumbbells come in two basic varieties\xe2\x80\x94fixed and adjustable. Fixed dumbbells will likely feel more secure and stable but provide only a single weight for each dumbbell. Adjustable dumbbells are usually bulkier and sometimes a little more rickety-feeling but provide a wide range of weights on one bar so you can build up to lifting more.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eDumbbells also come in several different materials, including rubber- and neoprene-coated models, and those made from unpadded cast iron, chrome, or steel. The former two types will likely be more slip-proof once your hands start to sweat, and less likely to damage your flooring. But there\xe2\x80\x99s no real disadvantage to solid metal dumbbells if they have textured grips and you rest them on a workout mat.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eAs for weight choice, Hake recommends beginners first consider their budget and what they hope to accomplish. \xe2\x80\x9cPick an appropriate weight that is challenging yet will allow you to perform your intended exercises with proper form and technique,\xe2\x80\x9d she says. \xe2\x80\x9cFive to eight pounds is a great starting point.\xe2\x80\x9d You might not want to buy an entire set right off the bat. \xe2\x80\x9cIf workouts will be sporadic, a single pair or even a single heavy dumbbell will do,\xe2\x80\x9d she says. \xe2\x80\x9cIf you are aiming to really build strength and want more options, it may be worth investing in a set.\xe2\x80\x9d\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eShe says she personally started with a set of dumbbells in a range from 5 to 25 pounds, which sit on a dedicated rack. \xe2\x80\x9cI also have many clients and friends who love the \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.amazon.com/Bowflex-SelectTech-Adjustable-Dumbbells-Pair/dp/B001ARYU58/ref=sr_1_5?crid=6D0F8ACX83LY\\u0026keywords=bowflex+adjustable+dumbbells\\u0026qid=1640707621\\u0026sprefix=bowflex%2Caps%2C117\\u0026sr=8-5\\" target=\\"_blank\\" rel=\\"nofollow\\"\\u003eBowflex\\u003c/a\\u003e adjustable weights,\xe2\x80\x9d Hake says. tool.\\u003c/p\\u003e","short_title":"The 5 Best Miter Saws for Woodwork Projects","index_title":"The 5 Best Miter Saws For Home or Pro Use","introductory_text":"\\u003cp\\u003eThe first woodworking machine many people buy is a miter saw, for good reason. This crosscutting specialist lets you buy any off-the-shelf wood product\xe2\x80\x94from a deck board to a piece of trim molding\xe2\x80\x94and cut it quickly, accurately, and safely to length. That simple ability, to cut wood accurately to length, and also to cut the ends to a variety of angles up to 45 degrees, makes an endless range of projects possible, from picture frames and decks to outdoor furniture and skateboard ramps, and too many other things to list here. \\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eOther tools do these basic jobs too, but the miter saw beats them all in some way. It\xe2\x80\x99s safer and less expensive than a table saw, more accurate than a circular saw, and faster than a handsaw. Whether you\xe2\x80\x99re a fine woodworker, pro carpenter, or DIYer, you\xe2\x80\x99ll use your miter saw for decades to come, for both rough and fine cuts. \\u003cbr\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cblockquote class=\\"body-blockquote\\"\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eThe Expert: \\u003c/strong\\u003eDuring my 30 years as a woodworker\xe2\x80\x94both professionally and as a DIYer\xe2\x80\x94I spent 15 as an editor at \\u003cem\\u003eFine Woodworking\\u003c/em\\u003e magazine and another six as a contributor to a variety of home-building and woodworking magazines. I also remodeled three homes, built hundreds of projects, and wrote two books on the subject, and currently teach woodworking locally. Throughout my career, I\xe2\x80\x99ve used and reviewed dozens of miter saws, so I know what works and what doesn\xe2\x80\x99t. \\u003c/blockquote\\u003e\\u003ch4 class=\\"body-h4\\"\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eSliding or Non-Sliding\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/h4\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eThere are two main types of miter saws. The most basic type, sometimes called a \xe2\x80\x9cchop saw,\xe2\x80\x9d swings straight down on a single pivot. This simple, solid action provides excellent accuracy in a relatively less expensive saw. Newer to the game is the sliding miter saw, with a blade assembly that not only chops straight down but also slides on smooth rails, increasing the tool\xe2\x80\x99s crosscut capacity. Both types are attached to tables that pivot right and left, over 45 degrees each way. For bevel cuts, both types of miter saws also lean sideways, some in only one direction and others, called \xe2\x80\x9cdual-bevel\xe2\x80\x9d or \xe2\x80\x9ccompound-bevel\xe2\x80\x9d models, tipping both ways. Single-bevel saws are becoming less common, and there are none featured here in our best buys.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eIf you own a table saw (capable of making wide crosscuts) go with a non-sliding miter saw, which has less crosscut capacity but is generally more accurate and less expensive. These have 10- and 12-inch blades; opt for the larger one. \\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eRelying on the miter saw for all of your crosscuts? Consider a sliding model for maximum crosscut capacity. Most sliding miter saws are dual-bevel, so that choice is made for you.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eSerious DIYers or professional trim carpenters may want a 12-inch sliding miter saw, which offers the ultimate in crosscut capacity and compound-angle cutting but is also the priciest saw of the bunch.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp class=\\"body-tip\\"\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eGear That Makes the Cut:\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003e \\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003e \\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/home/tools/g38413972/best-scroll-saws/\\"\\u003eThe Best Scroll Saws for Making More Precise Cuts\\u003c/a\\u003e \xe2\x80\xa2 \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/home/a29035809/woodworking-tools/\\"\\u003eThe Most Essential Tools for Your First Woodshop \\u003c/a\\u003e\xe2\x80\xa2 \\u003ca href=\\"https://www.popularmechanics.com/home/interior-projects/how-to/g830/10-jobs-you-can-do-with-a-multitool/\\"\\u003e12 Ways to Use Oscillating Tools for Your Next DIY Project\\u003c/a\\u003e\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch4 class=\\"body-h4\\"\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003ePortable or Plug-in\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/h4\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eMiter saws are extremely accurate, leaving the ends of your workpieces smooth and square, and cutting perfect 45-degree miters for boxes and frames of all sorts, as well as any angle in between. They\xe2\x80\x99re also portable, which makes them easy to carry to where the work is happening, saving you countless trips back and forth to your workshop. \\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eCordless models are best if you\xe2\x80\x99re working at a construction site. If you work at home, the cord won\xe2\x80\x99t be a problem. In fact, you\xe2\x80\x99ll get more power, dollar for dollar, and you\xe2\x80\x99ll never have to worry about a battery giving out.\\u003c/p\\u003e\\u003ch3 class=\\"body-h3\\"\\u003e\\u003cstrong\\u003eHow We Evaluated\\u003c/strong\\u003e\\u003c/h3\\u003e\\u003cp\\u003eThe miter saw was one of my first tool purchases. It was a beat-up old DeWalt I bought from a professional deck builder, but that still had lots of life in it. After a blade change, it served me well for 15 years.
